***щемить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:щемить.html>щеми́ть</a> (12687)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щемить.html>щеми́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ščemítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to pinch <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to cause pain or discomfort by pressing strongly</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to smart, to ache, to throb
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1997</b>,  Андрей Юрьевич <a href = vnd.unilang:курок.html>Курко́в</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Andrey_Kurkov" class="extiw" title="w:Andrey Kurkov">Andrey Yuryevich Kurkov</a>),  chapter 44, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>Добрый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ангел.html>а́нгел</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смерть.html>сме́рти</a></cite>  | <cite>The Good Angel of Death</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>ма́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>того́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:насквозь.html>наскво́зь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вспотеть.html>вспоте́вший</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:волдырь.html>волдыри́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ладонь.html>ладо́нях</a> поло́пались <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> оголённая <a href = vnd.unilang:кожа.html>ко́жа</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:щемить.html>щеми́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:малейший.html>мале́йшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:соприкосновение.html>соприкоснове́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лопата.html>лопа́той</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Málo tovó, što ja byl naskvózʹ vspotévšij, tak i voldyrí u menjá na ladónjax polópalisʹ i ogoljónnaja kóža <b>ščemíla</b> ot maléjševo soprikosnovénija s lopátoj.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Not only was I drenched in sweat, the blisters on my palms had burst and the bare skin <b>smarted</b> from the slightest contact with the shovel.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1960</b>,  Василий Семёнович Гроссман (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vasily_Grossman" class="extiw" title="w:Vasily Grossman">Vasily Semyonovich Grossman</a>),  chapter 61, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>Жизнь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:судьба.html>судьба́</a></cite>  | <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Life_and_Fate" class="extiw" title="w:Life and Fate">Life and Fate</a></cite> | , part 1:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишь.html>Лишь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:иногда.html>иногда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>но́чью</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:возникать.html>возника́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:память.html>па́мяти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:седой.html>седа́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голова́</a> алекса́ндры влади́мировны, <a href = vnd.unilang:насмешливый.html>насме́шливые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тетя.html>тёти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:женить.html>же́ни</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:начинать.html>начина́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:щемить.html>щеми́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдце</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:охваченный.html>охва́ченное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любовь.html>любо́вью</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Lišʹ inogdá nóčʹju voznikála v pámjati sedája golová Aleksándry Vladímirovny, nasméšlivyje glazá tjóti Žéni, i načinálo <b>ščemítʹ</b> sérdce, oxváčennoje ljubóvʹju.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Only sometimes at night Aleksandra Vladimirovna's gray head, Aunt Zhena's mocking eyes rose up in his memory, and his heart, in the grip of love, began to <b>ache</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***щенок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:щенок.html>щено́к</a> (4551)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">щеня</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščenja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ščenę</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щенок.html>щено́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ščenók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щенок.html>щенка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щенок.html>щенки́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щенок.html>щеня́та</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щенок.html>щенко́в</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щенок.html>щеня́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>puppy</li>
<li><i>(wild animals)</i> cub, whelp</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> snot; son of a bitch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ах.html>Ах́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:щенок.html>щено́к</a></b>! <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>Да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:повернуться.html>поверну́лся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́е</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ax ty <b>ščenók</b>! Da kak (že) u tebjá jazýk povernúlsja skazátʹ takóje?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">You <b>son of a bitch</b>! How could you say something like that?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>ще<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>но́к</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3°b  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-щен-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ок</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***щепа.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:щепа.html>щепа́</a> (22418)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ščepa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*skēp-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щепа.html>щепа́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ščepá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щепа.html>щепы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щепа.html>ще́пы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щепа.html>ще́п</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">collective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> woodchips, kindling wood</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:щи.html>щи</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> мн. lt;м 4bgt;  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка) |  <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> ед. ч. <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:использоваться.html>испо́льзуются</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>Для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:усиление.html>усиле́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выразительность.html>вырази́тельности</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>чтобы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смешивать.html>сме́шивать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a class="mw-selflink selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:щи.html>щи</a></a> [I] <a href = vnd.unilang:часто.html>ча́сто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:использовать.html>испо́льзуют</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:написание.html>написа́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>двумя́</a> «щ»: <i>щщи, щщей, щщам</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> т. д.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́нии</a> «<i><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></i>» <a href = vnd.unilang:использоваться.html>испо́льзуется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образец.html>образцу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельных</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>ви́н</a>. ед. <i>ща</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>ви́н</a>. мн. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:щи.html>щей</a></i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> им.=<a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>ви́н</a>. пад. ед. ч. <a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:написание.html>написа́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мягкий.html>мя́гким</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знак.html>знаком</a>: <i>щь</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <i>щщь</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>Фо́рмы</a> ед. ч. (<a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:особенно.html>осо́бенно</a> им.=<a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>ви́н</a>. пад.) <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a> жаргонны, <a href = vnd.unilang:чем.html>чем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:целый.html>це́лом</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:кроме.html>Кро́ме</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>того́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:изредка.html>и́зредка</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:прежде.html>пре́жде</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ния</a> «<i><a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щека́</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:скула.html>скула́</a></i>») <a href = vnd.unilang:использоваться.html>испо́льзуется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> 4b <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нском</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>ро́де</a>: <i>ща</i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:щи.html>щи</a></i>, <i>ще</i>, <i>щу</i>, <i>щой</i> (<i>щою</i>), <i>ще</i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-щ-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>.

<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:щипать.html>щипа́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 6c//1a.  <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-щип-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***щит.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:щит.html>щит</a> (3550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">щитъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščitŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ščitъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shield</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*skeita</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*skey-to-m</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*skey-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut, separate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">štit</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Irish">Old Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga">scíath</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">scūtum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щит.html>щит</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ščit</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щит.html>щита́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щит.html>щиты́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щит.html>щито́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>shield</li>
<li>sluice-gate</li>
<li>panel
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щит.html>щит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:управление.html>управле́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ščit upravlénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">control panel</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распределительный.html>распредели́тельный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:щит.html>щит</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">raspredelítelʹnyj ščit</i> ― <span class="e-translation">switchboard</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>tortoise-shell</li></ol>

***щука.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:щука.html>щу́ка</a> (10548)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ščuka</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*skew-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to frighten</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">scēoh</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">sciuhen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щука.html>щу́ка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ščúka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щука.html>щу́ки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щука.html>щу́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щука.html>щу́к</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pike (any freshwater fish of the genus Esox, a relatively large, predatory fish)</li></ol>

***щупать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:щупать.html>щу́пать</a> (10942)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">щупати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščupati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">щуп</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščup</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a probe, a dipstick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare as well <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">छुपति</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">chupati</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to touch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щупать.html>щу́пать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ščúpatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пощупать.html>пощу́пать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to feel, to touch; to grope</li>
<li>to probe</li></ol>

***щуплый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:щуплый.html>щу́плый</a> (13424)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">щуплъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščuplŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">weak, pathetic</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ščuplъ</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">щу́плий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščúplyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">skinny, unattractive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">щупля́вий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščupljávyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be"><a href = vnd.unilang:щуплый.html>щу́плы</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">щúply</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">skinny, unattractive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">štíplý</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lean, slender</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">šťúply</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slender, thin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">szczupły</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thin, lean</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щупать.html>щу́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščúpatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to feel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; original meaning presumably "so skinny that you can feel the bones".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щуплый.html>щу́плый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ščúplyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)щупле́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)щупле́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> puny, thin and weak</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щука.html>щу́ка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščúka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щучий.html>щу́чий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ščúčij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>pike's (the fish)
